Accenture Innovation Challenge 2023 is open to undergraduate and postgraduate students (currently full-time students) of all years across all institutes in India.
Participants can register individually or in teams with at most 4 members.

07/08/23, 9:39â€¯am - HOD Sir: Google just released 10 FREE Generative AI CoursesğŸ‘‡

1. Introduction to Generative AI

https://lnkd.in/gWD78CW9

An introductory level microlearning course aimed at explaining what Generative AI is, how it is used, and how it differs from traditional machine learning methods.

2. Introduction to Large Language Models

https://lnkd.in/g4wdBKHu

An introductory level microlearning course that explores what large language models (LLM) are, the use cases where they can be utilized, and how you can use prompt tuning to enhance LLM performance.

3. Introduction to Responsible AI

https://lnkd.in/gXCNePhA

An introductory-level microlearning course aimed at explaining what responsible AI is, why it's important, and how Google implements responsible AI in their products. It also introduces Google's 7 AI principles.

4. Introduction to Image Generation

https://lnkd.in/gjjEGxcV

This course introduces you to the theory behind diffusion models and how to train and deploy them on Vertex AI.

5. Encoder-Decoder Architecture

https://lnkd.in/gesTXkgF

This course gives you a synopsis of the encoder-decoder architecture, which is a powerful and prevalent machine learning architecture for sequence-to-sequence tasks such as machine translation, text summarization, and question answering.

6. Attention Mechanism

https://lnkd.in/g2evVK5Q

This course will introduce you to the attention mechanism, a powerful technique that allows neural networks to focus on specific parts of an input sequence.

7. Transformer Models and BERT Model

https://lnkd.in/gveBJYq8

This course introduces you to the Transformer architecture and the Bidirectional Encoder Representations from Transformers (BERT) model. You also learn about the different tasks that BERT can be used for, such as text classification, question answering, and natural language inference.

8. Create Image Captioning Models

https://lnkd.in/gnb83AXy

This course teaches you how to create an image captioning model by using deep learning.

9. Introduction to Generative AI Studio

https://lnkd.in/gc7sPExG

This course introduces Generative AI Studio, a product on Vertex AI, that helps you prototype and customize generative AI models so you can use their capabilities in your applications. In this course, you learn what Generative AI Studio is, its features and options, and how to use it by walking through demos of the product.

10. Follow ME on Linkedin

https://lnkd.in/eUWPnwXG

1.	Assessment consists of 60 MCQ Questions.
2.	The duration of the assessment is 60 mins.

Assessment Timings: Sep 18th, 10:00 AM - 12:00 PM 

Steps to attend Assessment:

Step 1:
Visit the URL, https://tinyurl.com/kaar-kovilpatti-25 and refresh the page once log in with your TERV credentials. If you are not a registered user click on Continue and do the sign up with your mail ID and Click Next to take the test.

Step2:
Read the instructions and click the checkbox, then click start Assessment

Step 3:
It's a Proctored test, So Configuration check for Video, Audio and Browser will be tested. 

Step 4:
You can click Confirm to save each question (If it's not clicked confirm your selected answer will not be validated) and submit the test after completing the test. 

Note:
This Assessment is proctored and hence you will not be able to take it up using any mobile device.

03/01/24, 3:42â€¯pm - +91 91590 90959: Dear students ,regarding University  elective courses registration process 1. If you  want to  unenroll some department  university  elective course, please write a request letter and get sign from your FA and HOD and submit the letter to concern department timetable incharge . Example ,if you want to unenroll waste water management course means, write a letter and get sign from your FA and HOD and submit your letter to biotechnology timetable incharge. 2. Example ,if you want to enroll some maths University course means, directly ,you can go to maths department and meet maths timetable incharge and enroll yourself. This is the steps you have to  follow for your university course enroll and unenroll process.  CSE students  no need to  meet our department timetable team. 28/01/24, 3:10â€¯pm - HOD Sir: The Principal/Dean/Director/Faculty

AICTE Approved institutions

Greetings from AICTE !

As you are already aware that Yuva Sangam is a flagship program of the Ek Bharat Shreshtha Bharat (EBSB) initiative, launched by the Hon'ble Prime Minister of India. This initiative focuses on conducting exposure tours of the youths comprising mainly students studying in Higher Educational institutions (HEIs) & some off-campus youths from one state to other states & vice versa. It provides an immersive experience of various facets of life, development landmarks, recent achievements and a youth connect in the host state. The program aims to promote national integration and understanding by connecting youth from different parts of the country through educational and cultural exchanges.

In addition to the cultural exchange, Yuva Sangam also includes a number of other activities that are designed to help students develop their leadership, sports and soft skills. For example, students may get an opportunity not only to participate in workshops on leadership, communication, and teamwork but also sports events that may be organised by SAI. They will also have the opportunity to meet and interact with VVIPs, celebrities or important personalities of the host state.

The success of earlier phases of Yuva Sangam are a testament to the importance of investing in youth and building bridges between different communities. The program has had a positive impact on the lives of thousands of youth and has helped to build a more united and inclusive India.

I request your support in motivating students of your institution to register for Yuva Sangam Phase-4, a student exchange program under EBSB. 

All interested students can register online at https://ebsb.aicte-india.org/

The registration has started on 25-01-2024 and the last date is 04-02-2024.

Please find attached a document on how to inspire students to register for Yuva Sangam.

PFA:- https://docs.google.com/document/d/14bG6HUV6Sm04-yG4vO5hph9CnBWpaHem/edit?usp=sharing&ouid=112998132956236016256&rtpof=true&sd=true 

Thank You
(Ravindra K. Soni)
Adviser, AICTE

Round 3:-

06/04/24, 12:44â€¯pm - Dhilipanrajkumar Sir: Dear IPT/Internship Coordinators

We have made few modifications for Internship approval process. This time internship registrations and approvals will be through Zoho Forms. Students whoever willing to go for internship will have to fill out a Zoho form entering their basic details, company and batch student details. Individual Registration is mandatory. In the form, Students must mention only their University Email ID . TPO will verify the company profile and give an approval based up on the verification. Students will get a mail notification about their applications status. If approved, students will receive an annexure along with the mail, which needs to be submitted with their department coordinator along with the company permission letter before they commence the internship. Department will conduct review only for the students who have successfully completed the internship and taken prior approval from the dept and TPO. Coordinators must submit the result passing sheet along with the students company permission letter and internship completion certificate with TPO. Result passing sheet will be signed after completion of document verification.

We have created separate forms for 2025 and 2026 passing out students.

*ISRO START programme* will cover various domains of space science, and the theme of the training is, 
*â€œExploration of the Solar Systemâ€*.
The START programme is a part of ISROâ€™s efforts to enable Indian students to become 
professionals in space science and technology, as the organizationâ€™s space science exploration 
program continues to expand into new domains. The programme is intended to provide students 
with introductory-level training in space science and technology, giving them an overview of 
different facets of the field, research opportunities, and career options.
The training will also emphasize the cross-disciplinary nature of space science, giving 
students insights into how their individual aptitudes can be applied to the field. The programme is 
expected to help build a human capacity that will lead space science and research in the future. The 
lectures will also cover topics on the Indian Space Science Exploration programme and research 
opportunities in space science and technologies.

05/05/24, 6:34â€¯pm - Murugeswati Ma'am: IPT/Internship Registration:

We have made few modifications for Internship approval process. This time internship registrations and approvals will be through Zoho Forms. Students whoever willing to go for internship will have to fill out a Zoho form entering their basic details, company and batch student details. Individual Registration is mandatory. In the form, Students must mention only their University Email ID . TPO will verify the company profile and give an approval based up on the verification. Students will get a mail notification about their applications status. If approved, students will receive an annexure along with the mail, which needs to be submitted with their department coordinator along with the company permission letter before they commence the internship. Department will conduct review only for the students who have successfully completed the internship and taken prior approval from the dept and TPO. Coordinators must submit the result passing sheet along with the students company permission letter and internship completion certificate with TPO. Result passing sheet will be signed after completion of document verification.

We have created separate forms for 2025 and 2026 passing out students. 

Registration Link

For 2025 passing out students - https://zfrmz.com/UQTPxTR7Ol0aC1yEFT2L

For 2026 passing out students - https://zfrmz.com/2X4TzkLWoRoFb6MiqLg1

07/06/24, 9:43â€¯pm - R Raja Course Cordinator: *IEEE R10Talk#5: Fortifying NIST Post Quantum Cryptography Methods on 8 June 2024*
Dear All,
Greetings from IEEE Region 10!
IEEE Region 10 Webinar Series "IEEE R10Talk" is pleased to invite you to its next webinar:-
2024 R10Talk #5: Fortifying NIST Post Quantum Cryptography Methods Against Unforeseen Mathematical Attack

Speaker: *David Schwaderer* | *IEEE Region 6, Northern Nevada Section Chair and CEO of ShapeShiftÂ® Ciphers LLC*

*Date: 8 June 2024 (Saturday)*

Time: 1:00 PM to 2:00 PM (UTC +8:00 / Kuala Lumpur, Singapore Time)
*IST Time: 10:30 AM to 11:30 AM*

Register at: https://ieeemeetings.webex.com/weblink/register/r93520cc0678a066e822c093f1b875a41

Abstract

The global Internet has begun a formidable migration to NIST PQC methods. Unfortunately, two of NIST's nine initial standardization candidates have already been cracked using unforeseen attacks. Because no remaining candidate ever will have a security guarantee, NIST recommends organizations develop operationally impractical, crypto-agile, hybrid data encryption solutions.

This presentation proposes overlooked, simple, Deterministic Chaos based data encryption methods that fortify and compliment NIST standards against such unforeseen attacks. Standalone, they stalemate all classical, Quantum Computer, and AI/ML mathematical algorithm racking attempts.

These mathematics-free methods provide provably unsurpassed data encryption simplicity, strength, performance, and safety.

The presentation will demonstrate a small, inexpensive, programmable cryptography module using them that encrypts data at approximately 2.5 GBytes/sec. using nearly obsolete cell phone technology.

*David* has 17 issued and pending patents involving a variety of system design and algorithmic methods. He has authored dozens of articles and eleven technical books that explain complex technology in approachable ways. David has developed six commercial software programs in several different languages for multiple machine architectures. He has delivered Usenixâ„¢  seminars on Erasure Coding, a subject he has presented several times at leading Silicon Valley conferences and enterprises. He has presented at Stanford, MIT, The Naval Post Graduate School, Google, Sun/Oracle Labs, and Samsung America HQ.

David lectures at Silicon Valley companies such as Oracle/Sun, Intel, and Google, as well as universities such as Stanford, MIT, and the Naval Postgraduate School, immersing audiences in his favorite subject â€“ innovation and its manifold surprises. His October 2007 MIT joint Sloan School of Management and Department of Electrical Engineering conference lecture was selected best in conference.

David has a Masters Degree in Applied Mathematics from the California Institute of Technology and an MBA from the University of Southern California.

Looking forward to your participation.

Thank you.
